    Roaming intranet easier (https://github.com/eddieivan01/iox)
Usage: iox fwd/proxy [-l [*]PORT] [-r [*]HOST:PORT] [-k HEX] [-t TIMEOUT] [-u] [-h] [-v]
Options:
  -l [*]PORT
      port to listen on. `*` means encrypted socket
  -r [*]HOST:PORT
      remote host to connect, HOST can be IP or Domain. `*` means encrypted socket
  -k HEX
      hexadecimal format key, be used to generate AES Key and IV
  -u
      udp forward mode
  -t TIMEOUT
      set connection timeout(millisecond), default is 5000
  -v
      enable log output
  -h
      print usage then exit
